talk</span></bdi></div></div></label></span></div></div></div></div><div class="mw-advancedSearch-namespace-2302 mw-advancedSearch-namespace-border oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-labelElement class="oo-ui-fieldLayout-field"><span class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-inputWidget oo-ui-checkboxInputWidget"><input type="checkbox" tabindex="0" class="oo-ui-inputWidget-input" value="2302" id="ooui-45"><span class="oo-ui-checkboxInputWidget-checkIcon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-check oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-iconWidget oo-ui-image-invert"></span></span></span><span class="oo-ui-fieldLayout-header"><label class="oo-ui-labelElement-label" for="ooui-45"><div class="mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget-label"><div class="mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget-label-title"><bdi><span class="oo-ui-labelElement-label">Gadget definition</span></bdi></div></div></label></span></div></div></div></div><div class="mw-advancedSearch-namespace-2303 oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-labelElement oo-ui-optionWidget oo-ui-decoratedOptionWidget oo-ui-menuOptionWidget mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget" aria-selected="false" tabindex="-1" role="option"><span class="oo-ui-menuOptionWidget-checkIcon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-check oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-iconWidget"></span><span class="oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-iconElement-noIcon"></span><span class="oo-ui-indicatorElement-indicator oo-ui-indicatorElement-noIndicator"></span><div class="mw-advancedSearch-ui-cell mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget-itemCheckbox"><div class="oo-ui-layout oo-ui-labelElement oo-ui-fieldLayout oo-ui-fieldLayout-align-inline"><div class="oo-ui-fieldLayout-body"><span class="oo-ui-fieldLayout-field"><span class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-inputWidget oo-ui-checkboxInputWidget"><input type="checkbox" tabindex="0" class="oo-ui-inputWidget-input" value="2303" id="ooui-46"><span class="oo-ui-checkboxInputWidget-checkIcon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-check oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-iconWidget oo-ui-image-invert"></span></span></span><span class="oo-ui-fieldLayout-header"><label class="oo-ui-labelElement-label" for="ooui-46"><div class="mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget-label"><div class="mw-advancedSearch-ui-itemMenuOptionWidget-label-title"><bdi><span class="oo-ui-labelElement-label">Gadget definition talk</span></bdi></div></div></label></span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-selectWidget oo-ui-selectWidget-unpressed oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-menuSelectWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-lookupElement-menu mw-widget-titleWidget-menu mw-widget-searchWidget-menu" role="listbox" aria-multiselectable="false" id="ooui-47"></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-49" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-48"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-50"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">These words</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for these words in the title or text.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>Multiple words can be entered here.</li>
<li>Punctuation marks and other non-alphanumeric characters (with exception of the colon and comma) will be ignored.</li>
<li>There may be results that do not contain one or more of your search terms.</li>
<li>Word stemming is applied. Example: If <i>car</i> is entered, the search will also consider <i>cars</i>. The word stemming is language specific.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Full_text_search">Full text search</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd><code>sesame street car</code></dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-53" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-52"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-54"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Exactly this text</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for a specific sequence of characters. Punctuation marks are ignored.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>(only valid when using quotation marks, see example below)
<ul><li>Separate the search phrases by comma or space e.g. <code>"good morning"</code>, <code>"hello friend!"</code>.</li>
<li>Punctuation marks and other non-alphanumeric characters (with exception of the colon and comma) will be ignored.</li>
<li>Search is not case-sensitive.</li>
<li>Word stemming is not applied.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Words.2C_phrases.2C_and_modifiers">Words, phrases, and modifiers</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words in quotation marks, for example <code>"Begin at the beginning"</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-57" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-56"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-58"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Not these words</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Excludes pages containing these words from the search.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>Word stemming is applied. Example: If <i>car</i> is entered, the search will also consider <i>cars</i>. The word stemming is language specific.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Words.2C_phrases.2C_and_modifiers">Words, phrases, and modifiers</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words with <code>-</code> before them, for example <code>-elephant</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-61" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-60"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-62"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">One of these words</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>At least one of the search terms has to be included in the page.</dd>
<dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Words.2C_phrases.2C_and_modifiers">Words, phrases, and modifiers</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words with <code>OR</code> in between them like <code>Laptop OR Notebook</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-65" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-64"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-66"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Page title contains</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for pages with titles that contain this word</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>The search includes redirects.</li>
<li>Word stemming is applied. Example: If <i>car</i> is entered, the search will also consider <i>cars</i>. The word stemming is language specific.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Intitle_and_incategory">Intitle and incategory</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words with <code>intitle:</code> before them like <code>intitle:queen</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-69" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-68"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-70"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Subpages of this page</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for pages that are subpages of this page.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>You can only search for subpages of one page at a time.</li>
<li>Don’t forget to enable the namespaces you want to limit your search to in the namespace filter.</li>
<li>Do not include the namespace in front of the page name like this: <del><code>Wiktionary:Redirect</code></del>.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#subpageof">Subpageof</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd><code>subpageof:</code> followed by a page name like <code>subpageof:Redirect</code>. Use double quotes if the parent page contains spaces: <code>subpageof:"Requests for comment"</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-74" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-73"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-75"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Pages in these categories</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for pages that are in these categories and subcategories.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>Only the first 5 subcategory levels will be included in your search.</li>
<li>The number of categories is limited to 256.</li>
<li>You can look for pages in multiple categories.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Deepcategory">Deepcategory</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd><code>deepcategory:</code> followed by a category name like <code>deepcategory:Help</code>. Use double quotes if the name contains spaces: <code>deepcategory:"Hidden categories"</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-79" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-78"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-80"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Pages with these templates</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches for pages that contain exactly these templates.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>You can find transcluded templates (templates consisting of other templates).</li>
<li>The autosuggest function can only find templates which start the same way as your search e.g. a search for <code>"com..."</code> will suggest <i>"commons"</i> but not <i>"nowcommons"</i>.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Hastemplate">Hastemplate</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words in quotation marks with <code>hastemplate:</code> before them like <code>hastemplate:"missing information"</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-selectWidget oo-ui-selectWidget-unpressed oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-menuSelectWidget oo-ui-element-hidden" tabindex="-1" role="option"><span class="oo-ui-menuOptionWidget-checkIcon oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-check oo-ui-labelElement-invisible oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-84" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-83"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-85"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">File type</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Searches only for files of the selected type.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>You can only search for one file type.</li>
<li>You can only select the given file types from the drop-down menu.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help pages</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#filetype">Filetype</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#filemime">filemime</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Words with <code>filetype:</code> before them like <code>filetype:ogg</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-89" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-88"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-90"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">File width in pixels</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>These fields allow you to specify the width of the file.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>This is only applicable to file types that have width and height, like videos and images.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#File_measures">Filemeasures</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Numbers with <code>filew</code> before them like <code>filew:&gt;800</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-94" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-93"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-95"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">File height in pixels</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>These fields allow you to specify the height of the file.</dd>
<dt>Be aware of the following</dt>
<dd>
<ul><li>This is only applicable to file types that have width and height, like videos and images.</li></ul></dd></dl>
<dl><dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#File_measures">Filemeasures</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>Numbers with <code>fileh</code> before them like <code>fileh:&gt;600</code>.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-anchor"></div></div><div class="oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-floatableElement-floatable oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored oo-ui-popupWidget-anchored-undefined oo-ui-popupWidget oo-ui-element-hidden oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-popup oo-ui-popupButtonWidget-frameless-popup" id="ooui-99" role="dialog" aria-describedby="ooui-98"><div class="oo-ui-popupWidget-popup"><div class="oo-ui-clippableElement-clippable oo-ui-popupWidget-body oo-ui-popupWidget-body-padded" id="ooui-100"><h6 class="mw-advancedSearch-tooltip-head">Sorting order</h6><dl><dt>Description</dt>
<dd>Change the sorting order of results. The standard is that most relevant pages are placed on top of the results.</dd>
<dt>Help page</dt>
<dd><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Help:CirrusSearch#Explicit_sort_orders">Explicit sort orders</a></dd>
<dt>Syntax-equivalent in the normal search</dt>
<dd>This feature has no keyword that you can type in the search input field since the function is specified via a parameter in the URL.</dd></dl></div></div><div
